Let's Logic Collection ID: 204
Title: Svens Collection
Author: Sven Egevad
Description: Sven Egevads collection The levels are in chronological order. Levels 1-49 were made in 1992, in the old Sokoban, and 50- made 2000 and later in Notepad. All tested in Sokomind. I have made a minor change in level 525, because it was a mirrored copy of level 522. (I thanks George Petrov for his observation.)
